[30;1m851 | [0m[35m## Always `schema`, never `database`[0m
[30;1m852 | [0m[35m[0m
[30;1m853 | [0m[35mApache Spark uses the terms "schema" and "database" interchangeably. dbt understands[0m
[30;1m854 | [0m[35m`database` to exist at a higher level than `schema`. As such, you should _never_[0m
[30;1m855 | [0m[35muse or set `database` as a node config or in the target profile when running dbt-glue.[0m
[30;1m856 | [0m[35m[0m
[30;1m857 | [0m[35mIf you want to control the schema/database in which dbt will materialize models,[0m
